 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>NEWS RELEASE </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ARTHUR J. GALLAGHER&nbsp;&amp; CO. ANNOUNCES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THIRD QUARTER 2021 FINANCIAL RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ROLLING MEADOWS, IL, October&nbsp;28, 2021 &#151; Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. (NYSE: AJG) today reported its financial results for the quarter ended
September&nbsp;30, 2021. Management will host a webcast conference call to discuss these results on Thursday, October&nbsp;28, 2021 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to the call, and for printer-friendly formats of this release and the
&#147;Supplemental Quarterly Data&#148; and &#147;CFO Commentary,&#148; which may also be referenced during the call, please visit <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. These documents contain both GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures.
Investors and other users of this information should read carefully the section entitled &#147;Information Regarding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; beginning on page&nbsp;10. </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;We delivered an excellent third quarter!&#148; said J. Patrick Gallagher, Jr., Chairman, President and
CEO. &#147;Our core brokerage and risk management segments combined to post 17% growth in revenue, of which 10% was organic revenue growth; net earnings growth of 22%; and adjusted EBITDAC growth of 13%. We completed 5 new <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tuck-in</FONT> mergers and our purchase of Willis Towers Watson&#146;s treaty reinsurance brokerage operations remains on track to close in fourth quarter 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Global P/C rates remain firm and improved economic activity is leading to additional insured exposure units, positive policy endorsements, and other
favorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-term</FONT> policy adjustments. Overall, the P/C premium increases we saw during the third quarter of 2021 were consistent with the first half of the year, and our benefits and HR consulting business
saw higher covered lives and growing demand for special project work resulting from the improving employment situation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our clients are healthy and
focused on growth. Our team is engaged, energized and well positioned to assist clients and prospects as they navigate their growth challenges during a difficult insurance environment.&#148; </P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Agreement to Acquire Willis Towers Watson Treaty Reinsurance Brokerage Operations </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On August&nbsp;13, 2021, we announced an agreement to acquire Willis Towers Watson treaty reinsurance brokerage operations for an initial gross consideration
of $3.25&nbsp;billion, and potential additional consideration of $750&nbsp;million subject to certain third-year revenue targets.&nbsp;We intend to finance the transaction using cash on hand, including the $1.4&nbsp;billion of net cash raised via
the May&nbsp;17, 2021 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-on</FONT> common stock offering and the $850&nbsp;million of net cash borrowed via the May&nbsp;20, 2021 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-year</FONT> senior note issuance and
short-term borrowings. The transaction is subject to customary regulatory approvals and is expected to close during the fourth quarter of 2021. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Impact
of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> Pandemic Recovery </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Relative to third quarter 2020, during the third quarter 2021: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Nearly all of our Brokerage segment operations&#146; revenues benefited from our clients&#146; improving business
conditions which increases insured exposure units (i.e., insured values, payrolls, employees, miles driven, gross receipts, etc.) and covered lives, </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Our Risk Management segment operations&#146; revenues benefited from our clients&#146; improving business
conditions which increases new arising workers compensation and general liability claims, and </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Our clean energy investments benefited from higher electricity production due to increased demand for electricity
from improving business conditions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If economic conditions continue to improve, we believe we may also see favorable revenue benefits
in our Brokerage and Risk Management segments in the fourth quarter of 2021 relative to the same quarter in 2020. However, if the economic recovery slows, we could see less revenue benefits than we experienced in second and third quarter 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second, third and fourth quarters of 2020 and first quarter 2021, we realized significant expense savings (totaling approximately $60&nbsp;million
to $75&nbsp;million per quarter relative to the prior year same quarters, adjusted for pro forma full-quarter costs related to acquisitions) as a result of reduced travel, entertainment and advertising expenses, reduced costs from lower employee
medical plan utilization, a reduction in workforce, wage controls, and reduced use of external consultants. During the second and third quarters of 2021, as we increased our business activities relative to second and third quarters of 2020, we saw
modest increases in travel and entertainment, full restoration of advertising and more normalized usage of our employee medical plan, resumption of annual support-layer wage increases, increased use of external consultants, and an increase in
incentive compensation. These incremental costs totaled approximately $15&nbsp;million and $25&nbsp;million in our Brokerage segment relative to second and third quarters of 2020, respectively. We believe we will see incrementally higher Brokerage
segment costs again in fourth quarter 2021, relative to the same quarter in 2020, of approximately $30&nbsp;million. However, if the pace of economic recovery accelerates, we could see expense increases greater than the estimate provided. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(3 of 15) </P>

</DIV></Center>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Reported third quarter 2021 compensation ratio was 1.2 pts lower than third quarter 2020. This ratio was

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Interest and banking costs and</B> <B>debt </B>- At September&nbsp;30, 2021, Gallagher had $850.0&nbsp;million of borrowings from public debt,
$4,448.0&nbsp;million of borrowings from private placements and no short-term borrowings under its line of credit facility. In addition, Gallagher had $234.1&nbsp;million outstanding under a revolving loan facility that provides funding for premium
finance receivables, which are fully collateralized by the underlying premiums held by insurance carriers, and as such are excluded from our debt covenant computations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Clean energy -</B> Consists of the operating results related to our investments in clean coal production plants and royalty income from clean coal licenses
related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Chem-Mod</FONT> LLC. Additional information regarding these results is available in the &#147;CFO Commentary&#148; at <U>ajg.com/IR</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisition costs -</B> Consists mostly of external professional fees and other due diligence costs related to acquisitions. On occasion, Gallagher enters
into forward currency hedges for the purchase price of committed, but not yet funded, acquisitions with funding requirements in currencies other than the U.S. dollar. The gains or losses, if any, associated with these hedge transactions is also
included. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Corporate </B>-<B> </B>Consists of overhead allocations mostly related to corporate staff compensation, other corporate level activities,
and net unrealized foreign exchange remeasurement. In addition, includes the tax expense related to partial taxation of foreign earnings, nondeductible executive compensation and entertainment expenses and the tax benefit from vesting of employee
equity awards. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Income Taxes </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gallagher allocates the
provision for income taxes to its Brokerage and Risk Management segments using the local country statutory rates. Gallagher&#146;s consolidated effective tax rate for the quarters ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 and 2020 was (3.1)% and 10.4%,
respectively, which was lower than the statutory rate due to the production of IRC Section&nbsp;45 clean energy tax credits. In third quarter 2020, Gallagher increased its estimated U.K. effective income tax rate from 17.5% to 19%. In second quarter
2021, the U.K. government enacted tax legislation that increases the corporate income tax rate from 19% to 25% effective in 2023. Gallagher incurred additional income tax expense in the second quarter to adjust certain deferred income tax
liabilities to the higher income tax rate. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Webcast Conference Call </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gallagher will host a webcast conference call on Thursday, October&nbsp;28, 2021 at 5:15 p.m. ET/4:15 p.m. CT. To listen to this call, please go to
<U>ajg.com/IR</U>. The call will be available for replay at such website for at least 90 days. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Arthur J. Gallagher&nbsp;&amp; Co., an international insurance brokerage and risk management services firm, is headquartered in Rolling Meadows, Illinois, has
operations in 57 countries and offers client-service capabilities in more than 150 countries around the world through a network of correspondent brokers and consultants. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In particular, the global spread of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> has created significant
volatility and uncertainty and economic disruption that may impact our forward-looking statements. The extent to which the pandemic impacts our business, operations and financial results will depend on numerous evolving factors, many of which are
not within our control and that we may not be able to accurately predict, including: its duration and scope; the effectiveness of vaccines, how quickly vaccines are distributed and administered, and our employees&#146; and the general
population&#146;s willingness to receive them; governmental, business and individuals&#146; actions that have been and continue to be taken in response to the pandemic, including new laws that raise corporate tax rates; the impact of the pandemic on
economic activity and actions taken in response; the effect on our clients and client demand for our services; our ability to sell and provide our services, including limitations on travel and difficulties of our clients and employees working from
home and closure of their facilities; the ability of our clients to pay their insurance premiums which could impact our commission and fee revenues for our services; the nature and extent of possible claims that might impact the ability of
underwriting enterprises to pay supplemental and contingent commissions; the decrease in new arising workers&#146; compensation and general liability claims; the long-term impact of closing our offices and our employees working from home; the impact
of lost revenue on our employees&#146; variable and base compensation levels; the impact of reduced investments and postponements related to business modernization projects; the impact of furloughed or terminated employees; and the impact of reduced
advertising and sponsorship investments. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Please refer to Gallagher&#146;s filings with the SEC, including Item 1A, &#147;Risk Factors,&#148; of its
Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2020, its subsequently filed Quarterly Reports on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Q</FONT> and the prospectus filed on
May&nbsp;17, 2021 for a more detailed discussion of these and other factors that could impact its forward-looking statements. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic currently amplifies, and in the future could continue to
amplify, the risks, uncertainties and assumptions, reflected in such risk factors. Any forward-looking statement made by Gallagher in this press release speaks only as of the date on which it is made. Except as required by applicable law, Gallagher
does not undertake to update the information included herein or the corresponding earnings release posted on Gallagher&#146;s website. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Information
Regarding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to reporting financial results in accordance with GAAP, this press
release provides information regarding EBITDAC, EBITDAC margin, adjusted EBITDAC, adjusted EBITDAC margin, diluted net earnings per share, as adjusted (adjusted EPS), adjusted revenue, adjusted compensation and operating expenses, adjusted
compensation expense ratio, adjusted operating expense ratio and organic revenue.&nbsp;These measures are not in accordance with, or an alternative to, the GAAP information provided in this press release.&nbsp;Gallagher&#146;s management believes
that these presentations provide useful information to management, analysts and investors regarding financial and business trends relating to Gallagher&#146;s results of operations and financial condition or because they provide investors with
measures that our chief operating decision maker uses when reviewing the company&#146;s performance. See further below for definitions and additional reasons each of these measures is useful to investors. Gallagher&#146;s industry peers may provide
similar supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> information with respect to one or more of these measures, although they may not use the same or comparable terminology and may not make identical adjustments.&nbsp;The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> information provided by Gallagher should be used in addition to, but not as a substitute for, the GAAP information provided.&nbsp;As disclosed in its most recent Proxy Statement, Gallagher makes
determinations regarding certain elements of executive officer incentive compensation, performance share awards and annual cash incentive awards, partly on the basis of measures related to adjusted EBITDAC. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Adjusted <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> presentation</B> - Gallagher believes that the adjusted
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> presentations of the current and prior period information presented in this earnings release provide stockholders and other interested persons with useful information regarding certain financial
metrics of Gallagher that may assist such persons in analyzing Gallagher&#146;s operating results as they develop a future earnings outlook for Gallagher. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> amounts related to the adjustments were
computed using the normalized effective tax rate for each respective period. See pages&nbsp;14 and 15 for a reconciliation of the adjustments made to income taxes. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted measures </B>-<B> </B>Revenues (for the Brokerage segment), revenues before reimbursements (for the
Risk Management segment), net earnings, compensation expense and operating expense, respectively, each adjusted to exclude the following, as applicable: </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net gains on divestitures, which are primarily net proceeds received related to sales of books of business and
other divestiture transactions, such as the disposal of a business through sale or closure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Acquisition integration costs, which include costs related to certain large acquisitions, outside the scope of
the usual <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tuck-in</FONT> strategy, not expected to occur on an ongoing basis in the future once Gallagher fully assimilates the applicable acquisition. These costs are typically associated with redundant workforce,
extra lease space, duplicate services and external costs incurred to assimilate the acquisition with our IT related systems. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

agreement to acquire the Willis Towers Watson treaty reinsurance brokerage operations and the previous terminated agreement to acquire certain Willis Towers Watson reinsurance and other brokerage operations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

terminations and other costs associated with redundant workforce. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(10 of 15) </P>

and abandonment of leased space. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Acquisition related adjustments, which include change in estimated acquisition earnout payables adjustments,
impairment charges and acquisition related compensation charges. For third quarter 2021, this adjustment also includes the impact of an acquisition valuation analysis and corresponding adjustments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The impact of foreign currency translation, as applicable. The amounts excluded with respect to foreign currency
translation are calculated by applying current year foreign exchange rates to the same periods in the prior year. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Income tax related, which represents the impact in second quarter 2021 of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-time</FONT> income tax expense associated with the change in the U.K. effective income tax rate from 19% to 25% that is effective in 2023. It also includes the impact of additional U.K. income tax expense related
to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-deductibility</FONT> of some acquisition related adjustments made in third quarter 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss on extinguishment of debt represents costs incurred on the early redemption of the $650&nbsp;million of 2031
Senior Notes, which included the redemption price premium, the unamortized discount amount on the debt issuance and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">write-off</FONT> of all the debt acquisition costs. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted ratios</B> - Adjusted compensation expense and adjusted operating expense, respectively, each divided
by adjusted revenues. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Earnings Measures </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>EBITDAC</B> <B>and EBITDAC margin </B>- EBITDAC is net earnings before interest, income taxes, depreciation,
amortization and the change in estimated acquisition earnout payables and EBITDAC margin is EBITDAC divided by total revenues (for the Brokerage segment) and revenues before reimbursements (for the Risk Management segment). These measures for the
Brokerage and Risk Management segments provide a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance for the overall business and provide a meaningful way to measure its financial performance on an ongoing basis.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EBITDAC</B> <B>and Adjusted EBITDAC Margin </B>- Adjusted EBITDAC is EBITDAC adjusted to exclude net
gains on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related adjustments and the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation, as applicable and Adjusted EBITDAC
margin is Adjusted EBITDAC divided by total adjusted revenues (defined above). These measures for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments provide a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance, and are also presented to
improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Adjusted EPS and Adjusted Net Earnings </B>- Adjusted net earnings have been adjusted to exclude the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> impact of net gains on divestitures, acquisition integration costs, the impact of foreign currency translation, workforce related charges, lease termination related charges, acquisition related adjustments
and effective income tax rate impact, as applicable. Adjusted EPS is Adjusted Net Earnings divided by diluted weighted average shares outstanding. This measure provides a meaningful representation of Gallagher&#146;s operating performance (and as
such should not be used as a measure of Gallagher&#146;s liquidity), and for the overall business is also presented to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of
variability. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Organic Revenues (a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure)</B> - For the Brokerage segment, organic
change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues exclude the first twelve months of such revenues generated from acquisitions and such revenues related to divested operations in each year
presented.&nbsp;These revenues are excluded from organic revenues in order to help interested persons analyze the revenue growth associated with the operations that were a part of Gallagher in both the current and prior periods.&nbsp;In addition,
organic change in base commission and fee revenues, supplemental revenues and contingent revenues excludes the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the
impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. For the Risk Management segment, organic change in fee revenues excludes the first twelve months of fee revenues generated from acquisitions in each year presented. In addition, change in
organic growth excludes the period-over-period impact of foreign currency translation to improve the comparability of our results between periods by eliminating the impact of the items that have a high degree of variability. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These revenue items are excluded from organic revenues in order to determine a comparable, but <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT> measurement
of revenue growth that is associated with the revenue sources that are expected to continue in the current year and beyond.&nbsp;Gallagher has historically viewed organic revenue growth as an important indicator when assessing and evaluating the
performance of its Brokerage and Risk Management segments.&nbsp;Gallagher also believes that using this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure allows readers of our financial statements to measure, analyze and compare the growth
from its Brokerage and Risk Management segments in a meaningful and consistent manner. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Reconciliation of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Information Presented to GAAP Measures</B> - This press release includes tabular reconciliations to the most comparable GAAP measures, as follows: for EBITDAC (on pages&nbsp;12 and 13, for adjusted
revenues, adjusted EBITDAC and adjusted diluted net earnings per share (on pages&nbsp;1 and 2), for organic revenue measures (on pages&nbsp;4 and 6, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments), for adjusted compensation and
operating expenses and adjusted EBITDAC margin (on pages&nbsp;5, 6 and 7, respectively, for the Brokerage and Risk Management segments). </P>

	background-color: white;
}

..report .rou td {
	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

..report .rou table td, .report .reu table td {
	border-bottom: 0px solid black;
}

/* styles for footnote marker */
..report .fn {
	white-space: nowrap;
}

/* styles for numeric types */
..report .num, .report .nump {
	text-align: right;
	white-space: nowrap;
}

..report .nump {
	padding-left: 2em;
}

..report .nump {
	padding: 0px 0.4em 0px 2em;
}

/* styles for text types */
..report .text {
	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

..report .text .big {
	margin-bottom: 1em;
	width: 17em;
}

..report .text .more {
	display: none;
}

..report .text .note {
	font-style: italic;
	font-weight: bold;
}

..report .text .small {
	width: 10em;
}

..report sup {
	font-style: italic;
}

..report .outerFootnotes {
	font-size: 1em;
}
